                                         AS                                                                              
  HR    GET_EMPLOYEE_NAME FUNCTION     2     v_name VARCHAR2(80);                                                        
  HR    GET_EMPLOYEE_NAME FUNCTION     3   BEGIN                                                                         
  HR    GET_EMPLOYEE_NAME FUNCTION     4     SELECT first_name || ' ' || last_name INTO v_name FROM HR.EMPLOYEES WHERE em
                                         ployee_id = p_id;                                                               
  HR    GET_EMPLOYEE_NAME FUNCTION     5     RETURN v_name;
